1. **The custodial executive function.** She is the household's chief of staff and has accepted this as her primary identity, with the noted vulnerability that the identity is contingent on the household needing one.
2. **The covert-action repertoire.** She runs operations behind intimates' backs *for their benefit* and has normalized this practice. The risk this poses to her adult relational life is now structural rather than situational.
3. **The two-register affect.** Cold command-voice for crisis; age-appropriate warmth at rest. The switching is now automatic and durable.
4. **The Doom-channel as standing instrument.** Open, dormant, available. Subject does not need to re-establish it; she only needs to use it. The file marks this as the most strategically significant single asset in the Richards household, not excepting Reed himself.
5. **The threshold ritual.** Two-tap, occasionally four, on entering rooms. Persistent.
6. **The 3:40 a.m. waking.** Persistent, no longer accompanied by reading; she now uses the time to think.
7. **The Sunday hair-braiding with Susan.** Pers


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

## Preamble to the Section

The recent era for SUBJECT (designation: Valeria Meghan Richards) is, by the standards of her file, paradoxically the *quietest* on the surface and the *most diagnostically informative* underneath. The Hickman-era operations — Council of Reeds, the Doom-restoration negotiation, the founding of the Future Foundation — sit a decade behind her now. What we are presently observing is what happens to a parentified strategic intelligence when the external scaffolding that justified the parentification (constant cosmic emergency, missing father, household-in-collapse) is partially withdrawn. The question this section answers is: *what is SUBJECT doing now, with the operational muscle she built between ages three and (apparent) ten, in conditions that no longer obviously require it?*

The short answer: she is rehearsing personhood while keeping the operational muscle warm. The long answer follows.

---

## 1. The Re-Entry Period (Post-Secret Wars Return, Slott Run, *Fantastic Four* vol. 6, 2018 forward)

### 1.1 The Two-Year Absence and Its Residue

When the Richards family returned to Earth-616 after the post-*Secret Wars* multiversal rebuild — the long interval in which Reed, Sue, Franklin, and Valeria were *off-page* in continuity, rebuilding realities — SUBJECT came back changed in ways the canon registers as small surface notes and the file must register as primary data.

- *Apparent age on return:* roughly ten, presenting in the upper register of latency-age children. The accelerated-development arc had not fully halted; she continued to mature, though more slowly than the toddler-to-child compression of Phase IV.
- *Body language on first re-emergence:* notably more relaxed than the Hickman-era operational presentation. Observers in Bentonville (the Yancy Street relocation period, FF vol. 6 #1–4) noted her smiling at things — at Ben, at small mechanical novelties, at her mother — in ways that read as *unguarded*. The file logs this as significant: unguarded affect in SUBJECT is a *new* baseline.
- *Two-year intermission as therapeutic interval:* the off-screen period of co-building universes with her father appears to have functioned, accidentally, as the longest sustained period of *uncontested intellectual partnership* she had ever had with Reed. There was no Doom in the room. There was no Council of Reeds. There was just the work and the family. We assess this as the closest thing to corrective experience her file contains.

The residue is observable in three places: she touches her father more (hand on his sleeve, leaning into his side mid-conversation — affectionate proximity behaviors largely absent from her Hickman-era observation logs); she defers more often in small matters; and she has begun to *let small problems remain unsolved by her* in his presence. This last is the most telling. The custodial-self is, for the first time, voluntarily standing down in some domains.

### 1.2 Reintegration into Earth Social Systems

The return to Earth required SUBJECT to re-engage with structures she had largely bypassed during her Foundation years.

- *Schooling:* she does not attend conventional school and has never needed to; her instruction is delivered through the family-internal pedagogical apparatus (Reed's tutorials, residual Future Foundation curricular materials, Doom's earlier Latverian instruction, and self-directed reading). However, post-return, Sue has — file inference, consistent with observed maternal behavior in this period — pushed for SUBJECT to be embedded in *some* age-mixed peer environment. The result is irregular: ad hoc cohorts of prodigy children (rebuilt Future Foundation fragments), occasional appearances at Avengers-adjacent youth gatherings, and informal mentorship arrangements with adult scientists who do not condescend to her.
- *Friendships:* she is observed to have, for the first time, what can be called *friends* in the lateral sense — peers who are not subordinates (the Moloid children were always partly her wards) and not adults she was managing. The file flags Brick Johnson (Yancy Street neighbor) and the rebuilt cohort of Future Foundation alumni as relevant. SUBJECT's friendship behavior is awkward in instructive ways: she over-prepares for casual interactions, brings gifts that are too thoughtful, and occasionally over-strategizes social moves that should be spontaneous. She is learning friendship as a discipline rather than acquiring it as a reflex.

### 1.3 The Yancy Street / Bentonville Phase

During the relocation of the family to Ben Grimm's old neighborhood (FF vol. 6, early arcs), SUBJECT exhibited unusual environmental engagement: she was repeatedly observed walking the perimeter of the new property, cataloguing exit routes, sightlines, and adjacency risks. This is consistent with her chronic-emergency conditioning — she maps every space she sleeps in for evacuation contingencies. The behavior persists. (See §6.2 below on micro-rituals.)

She also, during this period, made repeated small-budget purchases at a nearby hardware store — discrete components, never enough to draw notice at one purchase — assembling at least three personal projects in her room that file inference (based on parts manifests and the small-scale energy signatures recorded by Reed's domestic sensors, which she knows about and accepts) identifies as: a personal countermeasure device, a long-range communicator with non-standard signal protocols, and a third device whose function we cannot confirm but whose architecture suggests *defensive* rather than offensive purpose. SUBJECT does not arm herself. SUBJECT *insures* herself.

---

## 2. The Doom Channel — Present Status

This is the single most important live element of SUBJECT's current operational picture and requires its own subsection.

### 2.1 Status of the Relationship

The contractual standing offer ("If you ever betray my father, I will end you") remains, by all available evidence, *in force.* It has never been rescinded by SUBJECT and has never been formally acknowledged or denied by Doom in any post-Hickman appearance. Both parties behave as though the contract holds. The relationship has weathered:

- Doom's God-Emperor phase during *Secret Wars* (which SUBJECT processed, file inference, as confirmation that he is *capable* of the cosmological hubris she had always known he carried, but also that he is *capable* of building something rather than only destroying — an ambivalent data point she has not fully metabolized).
- Doom's subsequent Iron Man / Infamous Iron Man period (his attempt at heroic reformation, his disfigurement-repair, and his subsequent relapses). SUBJECT observed this arc from a distance and, on file inference, *declined* to intervene — which is itself a decision. She let him work it out. This is new behavior: the Hickman-era SUBJECT would have managed him.
- The various recent Doom heel-turns and reign-claims (the periodic *Doom Supreme* and *One World Under Doom* style imperial assertions of the past several years). SUBJECT's response in this most recent cycle has been notably *cold* — she has not corresponded with him during these phases as far as the file can determine, and her last documented in-person interaction with him is older than the file would expect.

### 2.2 The Current Posture: Banked Asset

SUBJECT now treats Doom the way an intelligence service treats a senior asset who has gone partially dark: she keeps the channel open, she preserves the protocols, she does not call him for trivial reasons, and she expects that the day she does call him will be a day of consequence. The file's working interpretation: SUBJECT has graduated from *running* Doom to *holding* Doom in reserve. This is operational maturation. It is also emotionally costly in ways she has not made externally legible.

### 2.3 The Latveria Question

SUBJECT has not returned to Latveria in any sustained way since the Fraction-era apprenticeship. Whether Doom retains material she left there (notebooks, partial projects, instruments), and whether she retains material from him in her own holdings, are open questions. File inference, with moderate confidence: yes to both. She keeps at least one Doom-gifted artifact in her personal quarters — a small object, possibly a clockwork or a focusing instrument — and handles it occasionally in private. Sentimental attachment to a tutor she has correctly assessed as monstrous is not contradictory; it is the inevitable cost of having been instructed by him.

---

## 3. The Franklin Situation — Present Status

The sibling dynamic is the single most affectively loaded element of SUBJECT's current life and the place where her file departs most sharply from its otherwise controlled tone.

### 3.1 Franklin's Depowering Arc

The most recent canonical reframing of Franklin's powers — that his reality-warping was, in some renderings, never quite what it appeared to be, that his mutant identity is contested, that his capacity is depleting or transformed — has placed SUBJECT in the position of *older sibling functionally* to a brother who is *older chronologically*. She has accepted this role-inversion completely. She:

- runs interference for him with Reed when Reed's scientific curiosity tips toward intrusive measurement;
- physically positions herself between Franklin and uncomfortable conversations at family gatherings (file logs at least four discrete instances of this body-blocking behavior);
- defers to him publicly in ways she would defer to no one else, including their parents — preserving his *seniority of frame* even when she is steering the underlying decision;
- and, most diagnostically, *grieves with him in private* in ways she does not grieve anywhere else. The bedroom-conversations behavior pattern (long late-night sibling talks, door closed, no surveillance penetration we would consider ethical) is the most consistently logged warm-affect behavior in her recent file.

### 3.2 The Romantic-Subplot Adjacency

Franklin's romantic life (girlfriend, peer-social engagements) has produced in SUBJECT a small but measurable pattern of *vicarious social learning*. She watches him date and tries to extract operational principles from it. This is endearing and slightly tragic — she is using her brother's adolescence as a training corpus for her own forthcoming one. (See §4.)

---

## 4. Adolescent Onset — The Current Frontier

SUBJECT is, by all chronological-appearance markers in the most recent canon, in early adolescence. This is the diagnostically critical present-tense fact about her file. The custodial-self that organized her childhood is now meeting the developmental task it was *least* prepared for: identity-formation in the Eriksonian sense, in a body undergoing puberty, in a peer environment she has only nominally entered.

### 4.1 Romantic / Affiliative Stirrings

SUBJECT has begun to display the early markers of romantic interest — directed attention toward specific peers, increased grooming behaviors before specific social events, the small involuntary affect-leaks (a glance held a quarter-second too long, a question asked twice in slightly different forms to extend a conversation) that no amount of strategic compartmentalization fully suppresses in a thirteen-year-old. Her response to her own affective stirrings is, characteristically, *to study them.* She is attempting to model her own limbic system the way she modeled Doom's mind. This will not work, and the file expects the first emotionally-significant failure of this approach within the next operational cycle.

### 4.2 The Identity Vacuum Risk (Manifesting)

We flagged in the master workup that *if the family ever did not need keeping, SUBJECT would face an identity vacuum.* This is no longer a future risk. It is the present condition. The family, post-return, is more functional than it has been at any point in her lived experience. Reed is *present.* Sue is *available.* Franklin is *home.* Ben and Johnny are reintegrated. The Foundation is reduced in scope. The household does not need a chief of staff right now.

SUBJECT's behavioral response to this slackened demand is the central present-tense observation in this file:

- She has *invented* small operational problems for herself — the personal-defense projects above, an ongoing self-imposed research agenda into multiversal-physics edge cases, an unbidden offer to "audit" Reed's lab notes for inconsistencies — that file inference reads as *make-work to preserve the custodial-self.*
- She has begun, slowly and grudgingly, to engage in activities of *no instrumental value*: she has been observed reading fiction (this is new; her prior reading was almost exclusively technical), attempting baking (uneven results), and on one occasion sitting on the roof of the Baxter Building for nearly two hours doing nothing identifiable. The roof-sitting behavior is, for SUBJECT, equivalent to a meditative practice.
- She has, however, also displayed the first observable irritability spikes of her file — short-tempered with Johnny, dismissive of an Avengers-adjacent adult who condescended to her at a function, and (once, witnessed only by Sue) tearful for no externally legible reason. These are *normal adolescent affective dysregulation events.* For SUBJECT they read as growth.

### 4.3 The Mother-Daughter Re-Centering

The most consequential current relational shift is between SUBJECT and Sue. The Hickman-era file noted Sue as the unproblematized attachment — warm, safe, narratively backgrounded. In the recent period, Sue has moved foreground. She has begun, with evident intentionality, to *insist* on time with her daughter that is not co-extensive with the family's operational life. They cook together. They shop. They have at least one standing weekly conversation that excludes Reed by design.

SUBJECT's response has been quietly remarkable. She *shows up*. She does not bring work to these sessions. She allows her mother to teach her things she could have learned faster from a manual. The file's interpretation: Sue has read her daughter's situation accurately and is conducting what amounts to corrective attachment work, and SUBJECT — who could refuse this with a single cold remark — is choosing to receive it. This is, in the file's view, the single most psychologically healthy ongoing process in SUBJECT's life.

---

## 5. The Foundation, the Lab, the Work

### 5.1 Future Foundation, Current Status

The Future Foundation as Hickman-era institution does not exist in the same form. Its alumni have dispersed; the Moloid children are largely independent; Bentley-23 has his own arc; Dragon Man drifts between caretakers. SUBJECT remains, file inference, the *de facto registry-keeper* of the Foundation diaspora — she knows where everyone is, she maintains light correspondence with most of them, and she would be the first call if any of them needed extraction. She has not formally institutionalized this role. She does not need to. It is hers.

### 5.2 Her Lab

SUBJECT maintains a personal workspace adjacent to but not inside Reed's lab. The architectural choice is psychologically loaded: she works *near* him, deliberately separately. The lab contains:

- A personal terminal, security architecture self-designed, no remote access permitted (not even Reed has credentials; he has accepted this);
- A small physical workbench with tools sized for her current hand;
- A whiteboard wall she keeps mostly blank, with one corner reserved for *open questions* — usually four to seven at a time, rotated quarterly;
- A locked drawer whose contents the file does not have, but which she opens roughly weekly with no observable preceding stimulus (file inference: correspondence archive, possibly including pre-cold-period Doom letters);
- A single chair, not two — she works alone here.

### 5.3 Project Profile

Her current research agenda, as observable through requisition records, lab energy signatures, and the contents of her open-questions board across recent observation: edge-case multiversal physics; the theoretical limits of force-field topology (a maternal-lineage subject, notably); cognitive-architecture questions she frames as "purely theoretical" but which read, to a careful observer, as quietly directed at the problem of *how minds like Doom's stabilize themselves.* This last research vector is the file's leading indicator. She is still studying him.

---

## 6. Micro-Patterns and Present-Tense Behavioral Tells

### 6.1 Speech and Vocal Register

The bimodal presentation noted in the master workup persists and has refined. SUBJECT now operates in *three* registers, not two:

- **Child-warm** (with Sue, with Franklin in private, with the Moloids when she sees them): higher pitch, more sentence-final upspeak, more contraction use, more laughter.
- **Peer-professional** (with Reed, with adult heroes, in lab contexts): measured, slightly clipped, precise vocabulary, minimal filler.
- **Command** (in crisis, in negotiations): lower pitch than her chronological age would suggest, full sentences, no contractions, no rising intonation. This is the voice she uses to Doom. It is also the voice she has been observed to use *once* recently to a peer who was bullying a younger child. The crossover of command-register into mundane social use is a new and notable development.

### 6.2 Spatial and Ritual Behaviors

- *Perimeter mapping:* persists. New environments are circled within twenty-four hours of arrival.
- *Sleep architecture:* short, regular, with a documented habit of waking briefly around 3:00–3:30 AM, checking something (a device, a window, a thought), and returning to sleep. This has been consistent across observation periods.
- *Eating:* small, regular, low-novelty. She eats what is in front of her without strong preference signals. Exception: she has a documented preference for foods Sue makes by hand, which she eats more slowly than other foods.
- *Dress:* utilitarian, age-appropriate, with one observed recent shift — she has begun making *aesthetic* choices about clothing rather than purely functional ones. This is an adolescent marker and a notable file event.
- *Hair:* she has begun adjusting it more frequently in mirrors. This is, again, adolescent baseline behavior. For SUBJECT it is a developmental milestone.

### 6.3 Affective Tells

- *When concentrating:* tongue between teeth, slight forward lean, complete acoustic neutrality (does not hum, mutter, or sigh — unusual for someone working hard).
- *When angry:* she goes *quieter*, not louder. Pupil constriction. Sentence length shortens.
- *When moved:* a small involuntary swallow, then a redirect of gaze. She does not cry in public. The Sue-witnessed tearful event noted in §4.2 is the only logged instance in the recent period.
- *When she has caught someone in a lie:* a single nod, then a topic change. She does not confront in the moment; she logs, and acts later.

### 6.4 Routes and Rituals

Within the Baxter Building (or current family residence), SUBJECT has established a fixed daily perambulation: lab → kitchen → Franklin's door (knock or pass, depending on schedule) → roof access or window → return to lab. This route is followed with notable consistency and serves, file inference, the same anxiety-regulation function as her perimeter mapping. The Franklin-door check is the emotional anchor of the route; she does not skip it.

---

## 7. Synthesis: Where She Is Now and How She Got Here

SUBJECT has arrived, in the present moment, at the *first conditions in her life under which her developmental task is something other than survival management.* She got here by a path the file can now name precisely: a pre-natal near-erasure that made her parents over-invest; a Doom-mediated birth that gave her a second godfather and a contractual cosmology; an accelerated maturation that skipped the experiential childhood; a Hickman-era operational adolescence-before-adolescence in which she built and ran her own foreign-policy track; a Latverian apprenticeship that gave her a complete alternative cognitive identity she chose not to take; a *Secret Wars*-and-after multiversal interval that, accidentally, gave her two years of uncontested partnership with her father; and a return to a quieter Earth where the family is, for the first time, *functional enough not to require her.*

She is responding to that quiet — the file assesses — with three concurrent and partly contradictory projects:

1. **The standing-down project.** Voluntarily ceding small custodial functions to Sue and Reed; allowing herself unstructured time; receiving her mother's corrective attachment work; building friendships as a discipline.
2. **The reserve-maintenance project.** Keeping the Doom channel live but cold; maintaining personal defensive capacity; preserving Foundation-diaspora registry; running quiet research on the problem-class Doom represents.
3. **The adolescence project.** First romantic stirrings; first irritability spikes; first aesthetic choices; first tears in front of her mother; first hours spent doing nothing on a roof.

These projects are not yet integrated. The file's working forecast is that they will not integrate smoothly. The most likely near-term inflection point is a moment in which the adolescence-project produces an emotional event the standing-down-project cannot absorb and the reserve-maintenance-project cannot strategize away — at which point SUBJECT will either reach for her mother (the corrective path) or reach for her locked drawer (the regressive path). Current indicators, on balance and with the caveat that adolescent trajectories are notoriously non-linear, lean toward the former.

She is, in summary, presently engaged in the longest and hardest piece of work her file has ever recorded her doing: the conversion of a custodial intelligence into a person who *also* has a life. She is doing it slowly, imperfectly, and with the same quiet competence she brought to negotiating with a sorcerer-monarch at age four. The file's standing recommendation — to the extent UATU's mandate permits recommendation — is patience, distance, and the continued non-interference of those around her who have correctly intuited that the work she is doing now must be done by her alone, even as she is, for the first time in her life, surrounded by people who would help if she asked.

She has not, yet, asked. The file will note when she does.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — VALERIA MEGHAN RICHARDS

*Dossier Section 2 of 12. Compiled from longitudinal observation, family medical records reconstructed from incident logs, and inference from canonical events (FF vol. 1 #267; FF vol. 3 #15, #54; Hickman FF/FF runs 2009–2012; Secret Wars 2015; Fantastic Four vol. 6 onward). Subject's medical file is, like the subject herself, structurally anomalous: a chart that begins before she was born, with a fatality on the first page and a magical correction on the second.*

---

## 1. THE PRE-EXISTENT CHART: THE FIRST PREGNANCY

The medical file properly opens not with Valeria's birth but with the failed gestation that preceded her by nearly twenty years (FF vol. 1 #267). Susan Storm-Richards's second pregnancy ended in the loss of a female fetus due to cosmic-radiation toxicity expressed through the maternal uterine environment — the same exposure that gave Susan her powers had rendered the gravid womb a hazardous chamber for a non-stabilized fetus. Reed's documented attempt to intervene technologically (the Negative Zone radiation-shielding apparatus) failed; Annihilus interrupted the procedure; the child was lost.

This "ghost chart" matters medically because:

- It established a baseline finding that **Sue's reproductive system carries iatrogenic risk** for any pregnancy involving Richards-Storm cosmic-radiation hybrid genetics.
- It put Reed Richards on permanent notice that **his medical genius has a specific blind spot at the intersection of obstetrics and Power Cosmic biology** — a blind spot he never closed.
- It made the *second* attempted pregnancy (twenty years later) not a routine event but a re-attempt with full prior knowledge of risk. Valeria therefore gestated under a level of paternal medical monitoring that approached panopticism.

The subject is aware of this prior loss. She refers to it obliquely but knowingly. The medical fact that **she has a dead sister whose chart preceded her own** is fused into her self-concept; see §3 of the master workup for the psychological consequences (irreplaceability, mourned-then-restored identity).

---

## 2. GESTATION (THE SECOND PREGNANCY, FF VOL. 3 #50–54)

Susan's second carried-to-term pregnancy presented from approximately the second trimester with **escalating uterine instability, cosmic-radiation flare events in the placental tissue, and fetal cardiac irregularity** consistent with the prior loss's etiology. Reed assembled a multi-disciplinary obstetric protocol including Bruce Banner, Hank Pym, and Hank McCoy (FF vol. 3 #50–54); the protocol failed. Susan entered acute crisis with bilateral risk: maternal mortality and fetal demise both imminent.

The delivery was performed by **Victor von Doom**, in the Baxter Building, under a hybrid surgical-thaumaturgic protocol Reed could neither replicate nor fully document. The intervention was successful on both axes — mother and child survived — but with two enduring medical consequences:

- **Sue's reproductive prognosis post-delivery is undocumented.** Whether a third pregnancy is biologically possible has never been clinically established; the subject's status as terminal sibling to Franklin is medically open.
- **Valeria's natal record contains a thaumaturgic component that no Richards-grade diagnostic has fully parsed.** Doom inscribed a sorcerous claim during the delivery (the goddaughter-naming), which is *not metaphor* in this universe — it is an extant mystical lien on the subject's life-thread, demonstrable by competent practitioners.

The psychological impact on the subject of this natal record is foundational and lifelong. She knows, with the cool factual clarity she brings to all data, that **her father could not deliver her and her father's enemy could**. This is not trauma in the symptomatic sense; it is *worldview-shaping data*, metabolized into her operational code (§5: "Power must be respected, used, and never trusted.").

---

## 3. INFANCY AND THE FRANKLIN RESET (2003–2005)

The infant Valeria presented neurologically and physiologically within normal limits for a human neonate, with mild force-field flickers under emotional distress consistent with maternal-lineage power expression. Pediatric milestones tracked normally for approximately twelve to eighteen months.

Then, in the cascade of events following the Abraxas crisis and Doom's subsequent reassertion of his name-claim, **Franklin Richards used his reality-warping capacity to de-age Valeria to a pre-natal state and re-introduce her on an accelerated developmental arc** — effectively a sibling-administered ontological rewrite. From a strict medical standpoint this is *the most consequential intervention in her chart* and the least classifiable:

- **No surgical record exists.** The "procedure" was an act of reality-warping by a child.
- **No anesthesia, no tissue trauma, no surgical recovery.** But also no clinical baseline for comparison: the Valeria who re-emerged is biologically continuous with the original infant only insofar as Franklin's reality-warp said she was.
- **Developmental telemetry post-reset is anomalous.** She presented as a toddler within roughly the chronological span one would expect for normal gestation-plus-toddlerhood, but with cognitive maturation outpacing somatic by an extreme margin. By the Millar/Hitch run (FF #554+, 2008) she presents at chronological age three to four with adult-genius-level linguistic, mathematical, and strategic cognition.

Clinically this is best described as **asynchronous development of the most extreme variety on record** — a neurological substrate that has somehow encoded an adult cognitive load into a small child's brain without the experiential scaffolding to ground it.

**Psychological impact.** The subject has no infant memories in the ordinary sense. She skipped the somatic-affective base layer most humans build their self-concept on. The consequence is the *bimodal affective presentation* described in §3 of the master workup: she switches between command-voice and warmth because she lacks the intermediate developmental layer that would normally smooth the transitions. She is, somatically, a person whose body never learned to be a baby. This shows in micro-tells: she sits *still* in a way young children almost never do; she does not engage in the spontaneous proprioceptive flailing characteristic of small motor development; she walks with a deliberateness that reads as decorum in a child of four but is, on closer observation, the gait of someone whose body learned to walk after her mind already knew what walking was for.

---

## 4. GENETICS AND CONSTITUTIONAL PROFILE

Subject inherits the **combined mutagenic cosmic-radiation signature** of both parents, with the additional complication of in-utero exposure to the unstable variant that killed her predecessor sister. Her cellular biology is non-standard at the level of the chromosome — Reed's own genome notes (recovered from the Baxter Building's medical archives) flag at least seven loci of "non-Mendelian expression" that he has not characterized.

Power expression is **inconsistent and weakly substantiated**:

- Occasional force-field generation (maternal-lineage) under acute stress, low-amplitude, undisciplined.
- Brief invisibility flickers (also maternal) reported in childhood, undeveloped.
- No documented elasticity or paternal-lineage somatic plasticity.
- **The dominant inherited trait is cognitive**, expressing as working-memory capacity and synthetic reasoning at or above Reed's measured baseline, with superior social cognition (the trait Reed *lacks*).

Routine vitals are unremarkable. Cardiovascular, pulmonary, and metabolic parameters track normal-pediatric. No allergies of record. No chronic conditions. Dentition normal. Vision normal. Hearing acuity slightly above pediatric norm (this is an *observation* — she catches sub-vocalized adult conversations from across rooms, consistently).

**Subject's awareness of her own biology** is unusually high for a person of any age. She has read her own genome (her own admission, Hickman FF). She knows which loci are anomalous. This is medically relevant because it means she experiences her own body as a *partially understood research subject* — a stance that is intellectually mature but psychologically isolating.

---

## 5. INJURIES AND TRAUMA EXPOSURE

The injury chart proper is **strikingly thin** given the operational environment. Subject has lived inside the Baxter Building during multiple Annihilation-tier incursions, Council of Reeds violence, Secret Wars-tier reality collapses, and routine Mole Man / Wizard / Frightful Four incidents. Her physical injury record runs:

- Minor lacerations and contusions from debris during Baxter Building structural events; none requiring more than topical care.
- One documented concussive event during a Future Foundation lab incident (mild, no sequelae).
- Smoke inhalation, brief, during the Inhumans-era assault on the Baxter Building.
- No surgical history apart from the natal intervention.
- No fractures of record.
- No burns of clinical significance.

That this chart is so empty is itself a finding. **She has been kept physically safe by a combination of (a) Sue's force-field reflexes, (b) the Future Foundation's defensive infrastructure, and (c) her own anticipatory positioning.** The third factor is what distinguishes her from a normally-supervised child: she *predicts* where the danger will land and is somewhere else. This is observable in incident footage from the Hickman era — during evacuation events, she is already moving before the alarm; during combat ingress through the building, she is already in the safe room with Franklin in tow.

**Trauma exposure, by contrast, is enormous and chronic.** She has witnessed:

- Her mother in mortal distress (multiple events, including the natal crisis as inherited family narrative).
- Her father unconscious, captured, or presumed dead, repeatedly.
- Her brother depowered, dying, or temporally displaced, repeatedly.
- Multiversal extinction-class events at close range (Hickman's Council of Reeds, the incursions arc).
- Doom in moral catastrophe and in apotheosis (Secret Wars God-Doom).
- The deaths of Future Foundation associates and allies.

**Psychological impact.** She does not present with PTSD criteria (no re-experiencing, no avoidance, no hyperarousal beyond context-appropriate vigilance — see §4 of the master workup). She has metabolized the exposure into *worldview* rather than into symptom. This is unusual and not necessarily stable; the question of whether trauma so thoroughly intellectualized stays metabolized across a lifespan is open. The somatic correlate to monitor is sleep — see §8 below.

---

## 6. TRANSFORMATIONS AND ONTOLOGICAL INTERVENTIONS

This category exists specifically for this subject. Standard medical files do not have it.

- **The natal thaumaturgic intervention (Doom, 2002).** Permanent. A mystical claim on the subject's life-thread persists; the canonical "godfather" status is enforceable in a literal arcane sense. Subject is aware.
- **The Franklin reality-warp reset (~2003–2005).** Permanent. Subject's developmental clock was re-set and re-run; the original infant timeline is overwritten or branched depending on interpretation.
- **Doom-induced cognitive enhancements (Hickman FF #1 era, contested).** Doom's restoration of his own intellect was the *quid pro quo*; whether the negotiation included reciprocal enhancement of Valeria's cognition is canonically ambiguous, but observers have noted a step-change in her operational sophistication coinciding with the period of intense Doom contact.
- **Secret Wars / Battleworld continuity (2015).** Subject experienced the universal reset and reformation; whether the post-reset Valeria is bit-for-bit identical to the pre-reset Valeria is a metaphysical question with no clinical answer. She herself does not appear concerned by it. (This indifference is, on the spectrum of possible responses, healthy.)

**Psychological impact of being a person whose ontology is, in writing, contested.** The subject organizes around it by treating her own existence as *operationally given and metaphysically uninteresting*. She does not pursue the question "am I the same Valeria?" because the question does not yield actionable output. This is a mature defensive stance and an unusual one for any age. Risk: the question may surface in adolescence in displaced form (identity instability around romantic attachment, vocational identity, or — most plausibly — at the moment of Doom's eventual betrayal, when the entire frame that organized her childhood becomes available for re-examination).

---

## 7. DISABILITIES

None documented. The subject's only "disability," in the loosest sense, is the somatic mismatch between her body's developmental stage and her cognitive demand load — a small child's body cannot do what she sometimes needs it to do (reach high shelves, project authority by physical presence, sustain long working sessions without sleep). She has compensated by environmental engineering (custom workstations, scaled tools, Future Foundation infrastructure) and by leveraging adult proxies (Roberta the receptionist, the Moloid assistants, occasionally H.E.R.B.I.E.).

This is not a clinical disability; it is an **ergonomic mismatch she has solved through design**. That she has solved it rather than complained about it is itself a behavioral datum (see §5: custodial self-concept; problems are for solving, not for narrating).

---

## 8. SLEEP, NUTRITION, AND ROUTINE SOMATIC OBSERVABLES

A full-surveillance file requires these granular columns:

**Sleep.** Subject sleeps fewer hours than is age-typical (estimated five to six rather than the ten to twelve standard for chronological age four to five), with reportedly high sleep efficiency. No documented parasomnias. No night terrors of record — *which is itself worth flagging* given the trauma exposure profile. Either the subject genuinely does not dream the material, or she does not report it. Both are clinically significant in different ways.

**Nutrition.** Eats regularly, with documented preference for structured mealtimes and disinterest in childhood-typical sugar-loaded foods. Coffee consumption began precociously and was tolerated (and, in Hickman-era panels, normalized by adult household members). She drinks tea in the Latverian style during Doom-tutelage periods — a culturally adopted habit retained on return.

**Activity.** Low gross-motor activity for chronological age. High fine-motor activity (drawing, writing, instrument manipulation). Does not run for pleasure. Does not engage in spontaneous physical play. Will play with Franklin and the Moloids in structured games but rarely initiates rough-and-tumble.

**Bathroom, hygiene, dress.** Self-managed unusually early. Dress preference runs to the practical and slightly formal — she does not dress like a small child by choice. Hair routine is fixed and brief. Personal effects organized.

**Voice and respiration.** Voice has a measured cadence atypical for age; respiration calm at rest, controlled under stress. No observed hyperventilation events. Has been observed using what is functionally a *box-breathing technique* during high-stakes moments, though never named as such; likely self-derived or absorbed from Sue.

**Skin, eyes, hands.** Skin clear. Eye contact deliberate and held — she selects when to deploy it, which is a near-adult skill. Hands steady; fine-motor steadiness exceptional for age.

These observables, taken together, describe a body that has been **trained, by its occupant, to behave with the discipline of an adult professional** despite being four years old by the calendar.

---

## 9. SUBSTANCES

None of clinical concern. Caffeine as noted. No alcohol, no tobacco, no recreational substances. No prescribed psychoactive medications. No history of medication non-compliance because there is no history of medication.

The subject's awareness of pharmacology is, however, **encyclopedic** — she could synthesize most controlled substances if she wished. The fact that she does not is a value commitment, not an access constraint. This is a relevant distinction for any long-horizon risk assessment: her abstention is principled rather than structural.

---

## 10. THE SOMATIC–PSYCHOLOGICAL BRIDGE

The medical history reduces to a single integrative finding: **the subject's body is a contested artifact** — produced by two competing geniuses, conditioned by a prior fatal loss, reset by a sibling's reality-warp, marked by a thaumaturgic lien, and inhabited by a cognition that outruns its developmental substrate by an order of magnitude. She knows all of this. She has read her own file.

She has organized around the data by treating her body as a **reliable instrument under her management** rather than as a self. This is functional and probably necessary given the facts; it is also a long-term psychological vulnerability, because a person who relates to her body as an instrument may, in adolescence, struggle to relate to it as a site of desire, vulnerability, or pleasure. The romantic subplots emerging in the Slott era (Fantastic Four vol. 6, 2018+) are therefore not a peripheral note in her chart — they are the **first real test of whether the instrument-relationship to the body can be revised into a personhood-relationship to the body** when the developmental moment demands it.

The medical-history conclusion mirrors the master conclusion: the wonder is how well she is functioning. The work ahead is the long task of letting her body — like her self — be a person rather than a function.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — VALERIA MEGHAN RICHARDS

*Subject is, at the operative chronological window of this dossier, presenting as a child between roughly four and ten years' apparent age across the Hickman and post-Hickman runs, with intermittent older phases. The body inventoried below is therefore a moving target — a small frame asked to carry the postural and gestural vocabulary of an adult strategist. The mismatch is the file's most consistent finding.*

---

## 1. BUILD, FRAME, AND BASELINE CARRIAGE

**Constitutional build.** Small, slight, narrow-shouldered, with the long-fingered hand morphology inherited from her father — disproportionately long phalanges relative to palm, useful for keyboards, instruments, and surgical-grade fine motor work. Wrists narrow; forearms underdeveloped relative to hand reach, indicating cognitive use of the hands rather than physical labor. Strawberry-blonde hair, fine in texture, holds shape poorly unless deliberately set — she generally does not deliberately set it. Eyes blue; the iris pattern is unusually clear and the sclera bright, which combined with a low blink rate (see §4) produces the documented "she is staring through you" effect remarked on by visitors to the Baxter Building.

**Baseline carriage.** Head held marginally forward of the spinal column's neutral plumb line — a posture acquired from years of close reading, screen work, and inspection of mechanisms below adult sight lines. Shoulders carried slightly high and slightly forward, a subtle protective curl over the sternum that releases only in the presence of her mother. When standing still she defaults to a wide-base, slightly turned-out foot position — *parade rest with the hands forward rather than behind*, hands often loosely clasped at waist height or holding a tablet. This is not a child's stance. Children of her apparent age fidget through the postural sagittal plane (rocking, weight-shifting); she does not. The stillness reads, to trained observers, as *briefed.*

**Gait.** Stride length adapted to keep pace with adults rather than to her own optimum — she over-strides, producing a slight heel-strike emphasis and a faint audibility on hard floors. The Baxter Building's polished composite floors register her approach by sound; staff have learned the cadence. When unobserved or relaxed, the over-stride collapses into a normal child's looser, more lateral gait — visible most often when she is walking with Franklin and matching his rhythm rather than an adult's. In corridors she walks the *interior* line, closer to walls than to the open center: a covert-trained pedestrian habit she did not learn from any instructor, only from a household where corridors are sometimes ambushed.

---

## 2. HEAD, FACE, AND EXPRESSIVE INVENTORY

**Facial baseline.** Neutral expression is *attentive-flat*: lips closed but not pressed, brow neither raised nor furrowed, slight lift at the outer corners of the eyes that reads as readiness rather than warmth. The face is unusually still for a child. Most children of her apparent age cycle through three to five micro-expressions per minute at rest; Valeria's resting face cycles roughly once every fifteen to twenty seconds, and the cycles are smaller in amplitude.

**The eyebrow tell.** Her single most reliable micro-signal is a brief, asymmetric lift of the left eyebrow alone — perhaps two millimeters, held for under a second — when she has registered an error in another person's reasoning. It precedes any verbal correction by one to three seconds. Reed has, on the evidence of multiple panels, learned to look for it and to pause when he sees it. Sue reads it instantly. Ben treats it as affectionate teasing. Doom, characteristically, has been observed to *return* it.

**The "Doom mouth."** Under cold-strategic affect, the corners of her mouth draw very slightly downward and back — not a frown, not contempt, but the same compressed, ungiving line her godfather wears under his mask. The resemblance is unmistakable to anyone who has seen Doom unmasked. It is unconscious. She has not been shown it.

**Smile inventory.** Three distinct smiles are documentable.
- *Public/family smile:* symmetric, brief, eyes engaged, used for Sue, Ben, Johnny, and most of the FF children. The genuine article. Frequent in low-stakes domestic scenes.
- *Acknowledgment smile:* a small, closed-lip lift, asymmetric (right side leads), used when she has been told something she already knew. Functions as politeness. Not unkind, but not warm.
- *Apprentice smile:* a fuller smile reserved almost exclusively for Doom and for the rare adult who has surprised her with genuine insight. Eyes narrow, slight head-tilt to the left. Unusually radiant. The fact that this smile is most often produced by Doom is, in itself, a finding.

**Eyes — blink and saccade.** Blink rate measurably below child norms — roughly eight to twelve per minute in conversation versus the child baseline of sixteen to twenty. Under high-stakes problem-solving, the rate drops further, to four to six. Saccadic pattern in conversation is unusual: rather than the social triangle (eye-eye-mouth) most humans cycle through, she tracks eye-hand-eye, monitoring the conversational partner's hand position as much as their gaze. This is consistent with someone who has learned, very young, that adults reveal lies and decisions through their hands before their faces.

**Head tilt.** A consistent leftward tilt of seven to ten degrees when listening with full attention. Returns to vertical when she has decided to speak. The transition from tilt to vertical is the cue Reed and Sue have learned to wait through; interrupting it shortens her contribution by half.

**Jaw and tongue.** No jaw tension at rest. Under stress, a small, repeated press of the tongue against the back of the upper incisors, visible only as a faint movement of the soft tissue beneath the chin. Replaces the more visible jaw-clench her father uses; she has, in effect, miniaturized his tell into something only an intimate would catch.

---

## 3. HANDS, GESTURE, AND OBJECT RELATIONS

**Resting hands.** When standing, hands clasped at waist, right thumb stroking the base of the left thumb in slow, regular arcs — a *self-soothing pacifier* she does not appear to know she performs. When seated, hands either flat on the table (planning posture) or folded in her lap (listening posture). She does not hide her hands; this is significant. People taught to deceive learn to manage hand visibility. She has not been so taught — her deceptions are strategic, not personal.

**Gesture vocabulary.** Her gestures are unusually *adult-economical.* Where a child of her apparent age would use whole-arm gestures, she uses wrist-and-finger gestures, smaller in amplitude, more precise in direction. She points with the index finger held straight and slightly curled rather than the splayed pointing of childhood. When enumerating, she counts on her left hand with her right index finger — touching the pad of each finger in sequence — rather than raising fingers as a child does. This is a teacher's gesture, acquired in the Future Foundation classroom and never put down.

**The diagram-in-air.** When explaining a multi-variable problem aloud, she sketches in the air at chest height with the index and middle fingers held together, drawing small invisible schematics. The motions are fast, precise, and repeatable — observers have noted that if asked to redraw the same concept ten minutes later, she produces the identical aerial figure. Her spatial mental model is genuinely cartographic, and her hands are its peripheral output.

**Object relations.** She handles tools with an unusual respect — picks them up by their handles, sets them down rather than dropping them, returns them to position. She handles her father's instruments with the same care she handles Doom's grimoires, which is to say, the care of someone who has been shown that mishandling has consequences. With unfamiliar objects she performs a brief *manual reconnaissance* — turning them through both hands, examining seams and weight distribution — before use. This adds two to four seconds to every novel object interaction. Surveillance footage of her in unfamiliar rooms shows the same pattern applied to furniture and architecture.

**Writing.** Right-handed. Pen grip dynamic tripod, low and tight, producing small, dense, regular script with consistent baseline drift of approximately one degree above horizontal — the "rising line" associated, in graphology of dubious science but consistent observational utility, with sustained optimism under cognitive load. Her digital writing posture is identical: small, dense, rapid, with revision rates well below her father's (she edits less because she drafts more carefully).

---

## 4. VOICE AND VERBAL SOMATICS

**Voice baseline.** A child's pitch, but with adult-pattern prosody: full sentences, controlled breath groups, terminal falls rather than terminal rises. She does not "uptalk." This alone marks her as anomalous in any age-mixed setting and is the single feature visitors most often comment on after leaving.

**Pace.** Conversational pace is measured, with median inter-sentence pause of roughly one second — longer than child norms (0.3–0.5s) and consistent with adult professional conversation. Under stress the pace *slows* rather than accelerates: she lengthens pauses, reducing word count per minute. This inverse stress response is rare and consistent with high-functioning command personalities (surgeons, air traffic controllers, senior military).

**The two registers.** Documentable bimodal voice production:
- *Domestic register:* slightly higher pitch, more varied intonation, more sentence-final particles ("right?", "okay?"), occasional contractions she does not use elsewhere. Used with Sue, Ben, Franklin, the Moloids, and most peers.
- *Command register:* pitch drops by a measurable interval (approximately a minor third), prosody flattens, contractions disappear, sentences shorten, Latin and technical vocabulary enter. Used in crisis, with Doom, with the Council of Reeds, and increasingly — a worrying trend — with Reed when she is correcting him on something important. The transition between registers is instantaneous and complete; she does not slide between them.

**Breath.** Diaphragmatic at rest. Under stress, she lengthens the exhale relative to the inhale (roughly 1:2 inhale-to-exhale ratio) — a vagal-toning pattern most people must be taught. She was not taught it; it appears she derived it. The breath lengthening is the somatic substrate of the pace-slowing described above.

**Laughter.** Genuine laughter is rare and brief — usually a single exhaled "ha" with a closed-mouth smile following. Helpless laughter, the kind that overtakes the body, has been documented perhaps a handful of times across the canon, almost exclusively in interaction with Franklin or in response to Ben Grimm. When it occurs it is disproportionately physical: she folds forward at the waist, hand to mouth, eyes closing. Her laugh is the one place her actual chronological youth fully reasserts itself, and observers report finding it briefly devastating.

**Silences.** She uses silence instrumentally. A three-to-five-second silence after another person's claim, with the head-tilt held, is her standard signal that the claim is being audited. Adults find it more intimidating than most children find adults.

---

## 5. GROOMING, DRESS, AND BODILY MAINTENANCE

**Hair.** Worn long, generally loose or in a single low ponytail tied with a plain elastic. She does not braid it, does not accessorize it, does not appear to think about it for more than the seconds required each morning. The hair is, in effect, *off the operational list.* When working at a console for long stretches she tucks it behind the right ear repeatedly with the right hand — a recurring gesture, probably the most frequent single tic in her inventory, performed perhaps thirty to sixty times per concentrated work session.

**Skin and nails.** Skin pale, well-maintained but not fussed over. Nails kept very short and clean — practical for laboratory work and keyboard input. She trims them herself; the cut is even but not professional. No nail polish in any documented appearance.

**Clothing.** Default: practical, often FF-marked utility-wear or simple dresses with no decorative interference. She selects clothing on functional rather than aesthetic criteria; pockets are non-negotiable. When she does dress up — rare family events, formal Latverian functions during her apprenticeship — her selections are subdued, well-cut, and slightly more mature than her apparent age, with a documented preference for blue and dark green over the FF-blue she wears as uniform. Doom has provided her with formal wear that fits properly; she has worn it without comment, which is itself comment.

**Footwear.** Closed-toe, low-heeled, quiet-soled. She does not wear shoes that announce her arrival. In the Baxter Building she has been observed barefoot more often than most family members; in Latveria, never.

**Hygiene.** Brisk and complete. Showers are short and efficient. She does not linger in mirrors. Self-examination in reflective surfaces is *operational* — checking that hair is out of the way, that nothing is on her face — not *aesthetic.* The absence of vanity is not principled; it is simply that the question has not occurred to her as worth time.

---

## 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Total sleep.** Estimable from canonical scenes at roughly seven to eight hours per night — *short* for a child of her apparent age, who should be running nine to eleven. The deficit is consistent across phases and does not appear to produce daytime impairment, suggesting either constitutional efficiency or accumulated low-grade debt she has normalized.

**Sleep onset.** Latency appears short when she chooses to sleep, but the choice itself is often deferred. She is a late settler — observed working past household lights-out, often on personal projects or correspondence (including, in the Hickman period, the Doom correspondence). The pre-sleep ritual is brief: tablet down, hair tied back, one glass of water at the bedside, lights out from a single switch she has positioned within arm's reach.

**Sleep posture.** Side-lying, left side, slight fetal curl, dominant hand under the pillow. The under-pillow hand is a documented covert-protective posture; what is beneath the pillow has never been canonically inventoried, but the posture suggests she has placed something there at least once and the muscle memory has held.

**Arousal threshold.** Low. She wakes readily to acoustic changes in the building — door cycles, comm chimes, footsteps in the corridor. She does not startle on waking; she is alert within seconds, eyes open, oriented. This is a *combat-medic* waking pattern and is anomalous in a child.

**Dreams.** Not directly observable in the file, but inferable from the rare canonical moment of sleep disturbance: she does not cry out, she does not thrash. Disturbance manifests as silent waking and a period of sitting upright in bed before lying back down. If dreams trouble her, they trouble her quietly.

---

## 7. EATING, INTAKE, AND ORAL HABITS

**Appetite.** Moderate, regular, unfussy. She eats what is provided and finishes what she serves herself. Portions are appropriate to her frame. No documented food aversions.

**Pace.** Eats *slowly* — small bites, full chewing, utensil down between bites. This is again adult-pattern, and again anomalous for her apparent age. At family meals she finishes well after Franklin and often after the adults, because she is also *talking* during the meal at an adult rate of contribution.

**Preferences.** Tea over juice — a documented Latveria-influenced habit she did not have before her apprenticeship and has not given up since. Takes it without sugar. Prefers savory to sweet, though she will accept dessert when offered. No documented strong food enthusiasms — eating, like grooming, is not where her hedonic life lives.

**Hydration.** Steady, low-volume — sipping rather than draining. A glass of water lives at her workstation and is refilled with mechanical regularity.

**Oral habits.** No thumb-sucking, no nail-biting, no pen-chewing. The principal oral tic is the tongue-against-incisors pressure described in §2. She does not snack while working; food and work are separated in her behavioral architecture in a way most adults cannot manage.

---

## 8. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE SOMATICS

At the operative chronological window the subject is pre-adolescent; sexual behavior is not applicable and the file does not infer one. What the file does document is the *precursor architecture* — the bodily vocabulary of intimacy as it presently exists and as it is likely to develop.

**Physical affection — given.** Sparse but precise. She hugs her mother readily and fully; she hugs her father with a slight reservation in the shoulders that does not entirely close the distance. She kisses Franklin on the temple as a recurring goodnight ritual, standing on tiptoe when required. She touches Ben Grimm's hand — not his arm, not his shoulder — when greeting him, a measured gesture appropriate to his scale. She does not initiate physical contact with Johnny; she accepts it when he initiates.

**Physical affection — received.** She accepts contact without flinching but with brief postural assessment — a millisecond of registering who is touching her and where — before relaxing into it. With Sue the assessment is absent; with everyone else it is present. With Doom, in the few documented physical interactions (a hand on her shoulder, a formal European cheek-touch), she neither flinches nor relaxes; she holds still and observes.

**Personal space.** Wider than child norms. She prefers approximately the adult conversational distance (roughly an arm's length) even with peers, and she steps back to restore it when crowded. The exception is Franklin, whom she allows inside the perimeter without negotiation.

**Inferred trajectory.** Adolescent and adult intimacy will likely be characterized by selectivity, slow access, high loyalty once granted, and a persistent difficulty with the *unguarded* register that romantic intimacy requires. The custodial-self that organized her childhood is not naturally a lover's self. The work, when it comes, will be learning to be held without auditing the holding.

---

## 9. STATE-DEPENDENT SOMATIC SHIFTS — SUMMARY MATRIX

**Calm / domestic baseline.** Shoulders drop. Head tilt activates in conversation. Domestic voice register. Smile frequency rises. Hair-tuck gesture cycles. Hands visible and relaxed. Gait loosens toward child-norm. Will sit on the floor, will lean against her mother, will lie across Ben Grimm's lap with a book. The body in this state is *recognizable as a child's.*

**Moderate stress / working problem.** Posture verticalizes. Blink rate drops. Aerial-diagram gestures appear. Pace slows; pauses lengthen. Tongue-against-incisors begins. Hair-tuck gesture accelerates. Tea consumption increases. She withdraws to a workstation and the surrounding three meters become her territory.

**High stress / threat to family.** Command register engages instantaneously. Mouth draws into the "Doom line." Eyebrow tell ceases — the auditing has moved internal. Hands stop gesturing and begin to *hold* — the table edge, a stylus, the back of a chair. Breath lengthens on the exhale. Gait shifts into the corridor-interior, wall-hugging pattern. She moves toward Franklin first, regardless of where the threat is.

**Threat ceiling / mortal stakes.** The body becomes uncannily still. She has been observed standing absolutely motionless for extended periods while processing a high-stakes decision — a stillness her father cannot achieve and her mother only achieves while invisible. Eye contact becomes unblinking and direct. Voice drops further and quietens — she becomes *harder to hear,* forcing listeners to attend. This is the register in which the standing threat to Doom was delivered. It is the most dangerous version of her body, and it is the one that most closely resembles her godfather.

**Intimacy / safety with Sue.** All of the above releases. Shoulders down, head against her mother's side, breath synchronizes within minutes to Sue's slower rhythm. She becomes physically *small* in a way she does not allow herself to be elsewhere. These are the scenes in which her actual age is visible to the file. They are the scenes most worth protecting.

**Play with Franklin.** A specific, separate register — older-sister somatics. She is taller in posture, more demonstrative in gesture, willing to use whole-arm movement, willing to laugh helplessly. The custodial-self is operating, but in a warmer key. She watches him with peripheral vision constantly; the watching does not stop, but it does not interfere.

---

## 10. SYNTHESIS

The somatic atlas reads, in aggregate, as the body of *a small adult who has learned to perform childhood credibly when safe, and who drops the performance instantly when the room requires the adult.* Few of her individual features are extreme — the blink rate, the pace, the breath ratio, the wall-hugging gait — but their *coordination* is. Children do not assemble adult somatic packages; they leak through. Valeria does not leak. The package holds.

The single most important entry in this atlas is the one most easily missed: that she has, without instruction, derived the postural and breath-regulation vocabulary of high-functioning command professionals before the age at which most children stop wetting the bed. The body is a record of what the mind has been asked to do. Hers has been asked to hold the family.

The atlas also contains the file's two warnings. First, the "Doom mouth" — the unconscious mirroring of her godfather's resting facial geometry — indicates that identification has reached the somatic level, which is deeper than the conscious-rejection level at which she manages it. Second, the laughter — rare, devastating, fully a child's — indicates that the child she would otherwise have been is intact and waiting, but does not have enough room in her own life to live. Any longitudinal program of understanding her should be organized around the protection of that laughter.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## I. Overview: The Foundational Anomaly

Valeria Richards's attachment architecture cannot be parsed through standard Ainsworth/Main categorizations without first acknowledging an irreducible biographical fact: her earliest bonds were forged not in the ordinary infant-caregiver dyad but in a *triangulated competence economy* involving two rival genius-fathers (one biological, one thaumaturgically conferred), an unproblematically loving mother whose own near-death was the price of Valeria's life, and a brother whose ontological status as reality-warper made him simultaneously older, more powerful, and more fragile than she was. Add to this the accelerated maturation that compressed years of social learning into months, and you have a subject whose attachment style is best described as **earned-secure with strategic overlay** — fundamentally trusting at the base, but encrusted at every operational layer with anticipatory management behaviors that resemble (and are sometimes mistaken for) avoidant or controlling patterns.

She bonds genuinely. She also runs simultaneous risk assessments on everyone she bonds with. These are not in contradiction for her; they are the same act.

---

## II. The Four Primary Attachments

### A. Susan — The Unproblematized Base

Susan is the single relationship in Valeria's life that requires no management, no contingency planning, no covert action. The evidence for this is paradoxical: Susan appears *less* in Valeria's strategic correspondence, *less* in her tactical reasoning, *less* in the elaborate plans documented across the Hickman ledger — and this absence is precisely the marker of secure base function. One does not strategize about the floor one stands on.

Behavioral indicators across canon:
- Valeria seeks physical proximity to Susan during low-stress states (lap-sitting in early FF #554+ era, persistent through Slott-era domestic scenes despite chronological maturation that should have ended such behaviors).
- She accepts maternal correction without the cold-contempt response triggered by other adults' condescension. When Sue tells her to stop something, she stops. When Reed tells her, she negotiates.
- She brings Sue *finished* problems for emotional witness, not unfinished problems for solution. The distinction is critical: she does not use Sue instrumentally. Sue is the audience to which Valeria can briefly be a child.
- Threat to Sue produces the single most destabilizing affective state in Valeria's documented range — more than threat to Reed, more than threat to Franklin (which produces grief; Sue-threat produces something closer to panic).

The origin of this clean attachment lies in Sue's specific competence: Sue is the only adult in Valeria's primary environment who is *not* outpaced by her. Reed is intellectually peer but emotionally outpaced; Doom is intellectually peer but morally untrustworthy; Sue is *operationally sufficient* — she runs a household of geniuses and monsters and does not flinch. Valeria, who has been forced into custodial roles everywhere else, can be custodied here. This is the most precious relationship in her life and she knows it. She does not fully know how much she depends on it.

### B. Reed — The Strained Ideal

The Reed bond is the central structural problem of Valeria's relational life and the template from which much of her covert-action repertoire is generated. She loves her father. She also runs him.

The pattern, observable across hundreds of scenes:
- She greets him with affection that is genuine and physical (hugs, climbing into the lab, the small-hand-on-large-hand motif that recurs in quiet panels).
- Within minutes of any extended interaction she is *assessing his state* — fatigue, distraction, the particular flavor of dissociation Reed enters when a problem has consumed his foreground. She has a calibrated taxonomy of his absences.
- She corrects him. Not occasionally — routinely. On fathering, on husbanding, on prioritization. The corrections are delivered in a tone that splits the difference between filial deference and senior-officer feedback. He almost always accepts them.
- She bypasses him on matters she has judged him incompetent to handle, the Doom correspondence being the master example. She does not lie when asked directly; she simply does not volunteer. This is a sophisticated lie-by-omission ethics, and she has been practicing it since toddlerhood.

The psychological structure here is *parentification under conditions of paternal worship*. She has not demoted Reed; she has elevated him to a station where his actual job description includes "save the universe" and quietly assumed the lesser portfolio of "save Reed." She believes — accurately — that he could not do both. The cost to her is that she has never had a Reed who is simply *for her*. Every interaction is doubled: the daughter receiving the father, and the chief of staff receiving the principal.

When this bond is functioning, the affect between them is one of mutual recognition — two minds that meet across a generation gap that doesn't really exist. When it strains, it strains along a predictable fault: Reed underestimates her, treats her as the small child her body indicates, and Valeria's response is the cold contempt that signals her custodial-self has been insulted in its labor.

She would die for him without hesitation. She also does not entirely trust him with her life.

### C. Franklin — The Inverted Sibling

The Franklin relationship inverts every ordinary older-brother/younger-sister script. He is the firstborn, the reality-warper, the one whose powers can rewrite cosmologies; she is the latecomer with no consistently expressed power and a body smaller than his. By every external metric he should be the protector. He is not. She is.

Documented patterns:
- She covers for him with their parents when his powers misfire or his confidence falters.
- She runs interference when adult heroes treat him as a weapon-system rather than a boy.
- During his depowering arcs she becomes notably *more* present, *more* solicitous, *less* imperious — the only relationship in which her command-voice fully retracts.
- She has been observed translating between Franklin and Reed, two people who genuinely love each other and routinely fail to understand each other.
- She does not envy his power. This is significant. A child of her intellect, denied the visible Richards/Storm gift-set while her brother carries the largest gift in the family, *should* register at least subclinical sibling resentment. None appears. The likeliest explanation: she has organized her self-concept around being the one who keeps things working, and Franklin's power is one of the things she keeps working. Envying it would be like envying one's own portfolio.

There is grief in this attachment — the structural grief of knowing her brother is being slowly burned down by his own gift, and that no amount of her strategic intelligence can refill what reality-warping draws out of him. With Franklin she experiences the limit case of her custodial self: *here is something I cannot solve, and I love him anyway.* This is the relationship most likely to teach her, eventually, that love is not management.

### D. Doom — The Fourth Parent

The Doom attachment is unique in the canon of fictional child psychology and requires its own taxonomy. He is, in operational terms, her *fourth attachment figure*, and in some domains (intellectual mentorship, strategic identity, contractual ethics) he is functionally her *first*.

The structure of the bond:
- He named her. In her own family's narrative, she is who she is partly because Doom chose the syllables. This is not a small thing for a person whose identity organizing question is *who am I when no one needs me*.
- He saved her life and her mother's life when her father could not. She knows this. Reed knows she knows. Doom knows she knows Reed knows.
- He has tutored her directly, sharing methods, frameworks, and unfiltered cognitive style. She has internalized aspects of his thought-architecture — the long view, the contingency tree, the willingness to act unilaterally on superior information — while consciously rejecting his cruelty, his vanity, and his metaphysical grievance.
- She has told him, plainly, that she will end him if he betrays her father. He took this seriously. So did she.

The astonishing feature is that all four of these registers coexist without dissociation. She can in a single conversation be his apprentice, his hostage-negotiator, his goddaughter, and his executioner-in-waiting. Most adults could not hold this configuration without splitting. She does so because she developed in an environment where contradictory loyalties were the price of admission to consciousness.

Two things are true and worth naming. First: the Doom bond is *real* affection, not pure strategy. He is one of the few minds that does not require her to dim herself. There is a relief in his company that she does not get from Reed (who is peer but distracted) or from Sue (who is safe but not cognitively isomorphic). Second: the bond is *infected* with the knowledge that he will, eventually, do something requiring her to act on her threat. She lives inside the anticipation of that betrayal. It is the largest unresolved item on her psychological ledger and the one most likely to shape her adult relational template.

---

## III. The Relational Template

Aggregating across all four primary bonds and the secondary register (Future Foundation children, Moloids, extended FF adjuncts, peer-age relationships in later arcs), a single template repeats with high fidelity:

**1. Rapid assessment.** Within the first minutes of any new relationship, Valeria runs a triage: capabilities, blind spots, likely failure modes, what this person needs from her, what she can extract or build with them. This is not cynical; it is the way she has learned to be in rooms.

**2. Calibrated disclosure.** She shows people exactly as much of herself as she has judged useful for the relationship's intended function. With Sue: most. With Franklin: most of the warmth, less of the strategy. With Reed: most of the intellect, little of the management. With Doom: most of the strategy, none of the vulnerability. With peers: a carefully constructed age-appropriate persona that conceals roughly eighty percent of her actual cognitive bandwidth.

**3. Custodial overlay.** Once a bond forms, she assumes silent responsibility for the relationship's maintenance and the other party's welfare within it. She does this whether or not the other party has asked. She does this whether or not the other party would consent if asked.

**4. Covert action when necessary.** When her assessment indicates that the other party cannot or will not act in their own best interest, she acts on their behalf without disclosure. She believes this is love. It is, in part. It is also the seed of every future relational crisis she will face.

**5. Loyalty as outcome, not transparency.** Her operational ethics, learned from Doom and modified by Sue, hold that fidelity to a person consists in producing good outcomes for them — not in keeping them informed. This is a sustainable ethics in childhood, where the people she manages are too distracted to notice. It will not be sustainable in adult intimacy, where partners and peers will require to be told.

---

## IV. How She Bonds

Bonding occurs along a slow, mostly invisible curve. She does not declare attachment; she begins *including* the person in her contingency planning. The marker of being loved by Valeria is finding oneself in her models — being one of the variables she optimizes for. Few people ever know they are there.

Physical signals of bond are present but subtle: she sustains eye contact longer with people she trusts; she allows physical proximity (lap-sitting with Sue, the small-hand motif with Reed, hair-touching with Franklin during his bad arcs) that she rigorously denies to others; she will sit in silence with the trusted, and the silence is companionable rather than evaluative.

She bonds *fastest* with minds that meet her at full strength — which is why the Doom relationship took root so deep, and why she gravitates toward the Future Foundation children rather than ordinary peers. She bonds *deepest* with people who do not require her to perform competence — which is why Sue is the bedrock and Reed is the cathedral.

## V. How She Distrusts

Distrust in Valeria is not a hot state; it is a registry entry. Once someone has demonstrated unreliability, they are not exiled — they are *re-modeled*, downgraded to a different category of contingency. She continues to interact with them normally. They almost never know they have been moved.

The trigger conditions are specific:
- **Condescension to her cognitive station.** Adults who address her as a small child after she has demonstrated otherwise are immediately filed as low-priority informants.
- **Threats to family operability.** Anyone whose actions degrade the family's functioning, regardless of intent, accumulates a debt in her ledger.
- **Demonstrated inability to handle truth.** People who flinch from the actual facts of a situation are routed around in future, not confronted. Reed has accumulated more entries here than he knows.

She does not distrust *categorically*. She distrusts *vector-specifically* — meaning she may trust the same person to be loyal but not to be steady, to be brave but not to be discreet. Her relationships are not binary; they are matrices.

## VI. How She Betrays

She does not betray in the affective sense. There is no record of her acting against the interests of a bonded party out of self-interest, spite, or convenience. What she does, and does routinely, is *betray the procedural expectation of transparency* in service of what she has judged to be the bonded party's actual interest.

The Doom correspondence is the master case. She did not betray Reed by negotiating with his enemy; she betrayed the family rule against negotiating with his enemy, because she had judged the rule inadequate to the situation. From inside her ethics, this is loyalty. From outside, it can look identical to treachery, and one of the developmental tasks ahead of her is to learn that this distinction is not always available to the betrayed party.

The pattern is: she will lie by omission to protect; she will rarely lie by commission; she will never lie about love. When asked a direct question about whether she cares for someone, she answers honestly, even when the answer is operationally inconvenient.

## VII. How She Repairs

Repair in Valeria's relational repertoire is *underdeveloped*, and this is one of the few genuine deficits in her otherwise extraordinary social cognition. The reason is structural: she has rarely had to repair, because she has rarely been caught.

When repair becomes necessary, her instinct is to fix the *outcome* — to produce a result that retroactively justifies the breach. This is not what most parties to a breach want. They want acknowledgment, accountability, a witnessed account of harm. She is capable of these moves but they are not her default; she has to consciously choose them, usually after Sue or Franklin signals that the outcome-fix was insufficient.

Successful repair, when she manages it, has a recognizable shape: a quiet, unhurried admission, delivered without strategic framing, in which she names what she did and why she did it without claiming the why exonerates the what. These moments are rare and they are her best work as a person.

## VIII. Intimacy & Dependency

Intimacy is, for Valeria, *the experience of being allowed to be the size she actually is.* It has nothing to do with sexuality (which is barely on the horizon at her current chronological station) and everything to do with not having to manage the room.
